UPDATE
	PSIProgramPart prg
SET
	prg_mostRecentMADateWPS = (
		SELECT
			min(pic.PIC_MOSTRECENTMADATEWPS)
		FROM
			CM2ProductInContract pic
			INNER JOIN PSIProgramPart prog ON prog.PRODUCTPART = pic.PIC_ID_PRODUCT
		WHERE ( prog.prg_id_series = prg.PRODUCTPART OR prog.prg_id_parentSeries = prg.PRODUCTPART ) AND pic.PIC_MOSTRECENTMADATEWPS IS NOT NULL
	)
WHERE
	productpart in (
		select
			oid
		from
			PSIProductPart
		where
			PRD_ID_PRODUCTTYPE in (
				select
					oid
				from
					leafoftree
				where
					LOTTYPE = 571
					and (
						predefinedValue in (''Series'', ''parentSeries'')
					)
			)
	)'
